How to read this dashboard

ConceptPlain-English guide
Market SummaryMarket Summary = whether the market environment supports fresh long trades.
Daily TopDaily Top = conditional execution candidates, maximum four, never forced.
Weekly UniverseWeekly Universe = broader AURORA watchlist selected from full-universe discovery.
RSLERSLE = strongest relative-strength leaders with tactical entries or developing entries.
Sector / ThemeSector / Theme = row-level theme, sector, industry, and sector-RRG read. Sector context is a probability/tailwind guide. Leading or improving sectors usually support better odds. Weakening or lagging sectors require stronger stock-level RS, setup quality, and risk control. Sector RRG does not create or block AURORA trade buckets. LEADING = sector tailwind supports the setup. IMPROVING = early rotation; constructive but confirm stock-level RS/setup. WEAKENING = be selective; sector momentum is fading. LAGGING = lower probability unless stock-level RS/setup is exceptional. UNKNOWN / NOT_CALCULATED = sector data unavailable; do not infer. A lagging sector lowers probability but does not automatically reject a stock.
Table scrollingWide tables are scrollable left/right and top/bottom. Headers remain visible while scrolling.
Sector RRGSector RRG = sector rotation strength. Sector context is a probability/tailwind guide. Leading or improving sectors usually support better odds. Weakening or lagging sectors require stronger stock-level RS, setup quality, and risk control. Sector RRG does not create or block AURORA trade buckets. LEADING = sector tailwind supports the setup. IMPROVING = early rotation; constructive but confirm stock-level RS/setup. WEAKENING = be selective; sector momentum is fading. LAGGING = lower probability unless stock-level RS/setup is exceptional. UNKNOWN / NOT_CALCULATED = sector data unavailable; do not infer. A lagging sector lowers probability but does not automatically reject a stock.
Stock Theme LeadershipStock Theme Leadership = clustering of shortlisted stocks, not a buy signal. This table shows where AURORA candidates are clustering. It is not a buy table and not a trade signal. Weighted Presence = Weekly*3 + DailyTop*4 + RSLE*2 + Developing*1. Weekly = count from WEEKLY_UNIVERSE. Daily Top = count from DAILY_TOP_1_4. RSLE = count from AURORA-RSLE Top 20. Developing = count from Developing Watchlist. Symbols = representative stocks from that theme. India examples: Auto Components, EMS / Electronics, Defence, Capital Markets, Energy / Infra, Pharma / CDMO.
Stock rowStock row = final decision comes from bucket + setup + RS + volume + risk + market permission.
AURORA Bucket / SetupAURORA Bucket = final trade-readiness status. Setup = diagnostic setup lane explaining why the stock is being watched. Locked final buckets: TRADE_READY, TRIGGER_READY, EARLY_ENTRY_WATCH, PULLBACK_WATCH, RSNH_WATCH_ONLY, NO_CHASE, PROTECT_PROFIT_REVIEW, REPAIR_WATCH, AVOID_FRESH_LONG.
RS / RS21 / RSNHRS means benchmark-relative strength, not RSI. RS21 = RS line versus its 21 EMA. RSNH = relative-strength line near or at new high. RS Trifecta = RS confirmation stack. Mansfield RS = longer-term trend-adjusted outperformance.
RRG / RMVRRG shows rotation context. RMV shows reduced-move volatility/tightness context.
VE2 / PBX / BPX / BasePivot / RMVP / AXMVE2 = volume quality and demand/supply evidence. PBX = pullback quality. BPX/BasePivot/RMVP = structure, trigger zones, support/retest zones. AXM = ATR-based extension and no-chase risk. None of these creates a standalone buy signal.
Entry / StopEntry / Stop shows the reference trigger, stop, and risk that still need market permission and price/volume acceptance.
LiquidityLiquidity checks whether participation is sufficient before a setup can be actionable.
Caution / NextCaution / Next explains what must happen before promotion or execution. It may include volume confirmation, trigger acceptance, tighter shelf, pullback reset, data repair, or no-chase reset.

Column Guide

ColumnMeaningHow to Use
SymbolTicker, exchange, series, and source lane.Confirm route and whether the name is NSE core, restricted/caution, or BSE overlay.
User NotePlain-English reason the stock is on the list.Start here before reading the numeric fields.
Sector / ThemeAurora theme, sector, industry, and sector-RRG context.Sector context is probability/tailwind context only; it does not block, rank, or bucket candidates.
AURORA BucketLocked final trade bucket plus weekly/daily tier.Use this as the main trade-readiness label.
SetupDiagnostic setup label and entry permission.Confirms whether it is trigger-ready, pullback, compression, RMVP, or watch-only.
ScoreTotal, leadership, tactical, and weekly watchlist scores.Ranks candidates after all local calculations.
RSRelative strength versus benchmark: RS rating, 1W/1M/3M relative returns, RS21 and Trifecta state.Primary leadership evidence. This is not RSI.
RRGRelative rotation quadrant with ratio and momentum.Use as sector/stock leadership context; no direction labels shown.
RMV5/15/25-day range compression.Finds tightness, VCP-style contraction, and compression setups.
BasePivot / RMVPBase pivot, reduced-move pivot, base-count proxy, and shortlist pattern context.Defines nearby structure, early-entry pivots, and late-stage base caution.
PBXPullback depth, duration, MA defense, reversal and failure check.Grades whether the pullback is constructive.
VE2 VolumeVolume signature, dry-up, RVOL, distribution, and delivery confirmation.Adds conviction or caution; not a standalone signal.
AXMATR extension from key moving averages.Prevents chasing extended leaders.
Entry / StopEntry reference, tactical stop, and thesis stop.Use tactical risk for entry permission; thesis risk is context.
Liquidity20-day average rupee turnover and liquidity percentile.Thin names are cautioned, not automatically hidden.
Caution / NextMain caution and next promotion condition.Shows what must happen before upgrade.

Sector and Theme RRG

Sector context is a probability/tailwind guide. Leading or improving sectors usually support better odds. Weakening or lagging sectors require stronger stock-level RS, setup quality, and risk control. Sector RRG does not create or block AURORA trade buckets. LEADING = sector tailwind supports the setup. IMPROVING = early rotation; constructive but confirm stock-level RS/setup. WEAKENING = be selective; sector momentum is fading. LAGGING = lower probability unless stock-level RS/setup is exceptional. UNKNOWN / NOT_CALCULATED = sector data unavailable; do not infer. A lagging sector lowers probability but does not automatically reject a stock.

RRG Quadrant Map

ItemMeaningUser Action
LEADINGRelative strength and relative momentum are both above benchmark baseline.Best area to hunt entries if setup/risk are clean.
IMPROVINGMomentum is improving before full leadership is confirmed.Useful early-entry watch zone.
WEAKENINGStill strong versus benchmark, but momentum is fading.Avoid chasing; prefer pullback/retest only.
LAGGINGBoth relative strength and momentum are weak.Repair watch unless a catalyst changes behavior.

Stocks whose RS line is within 1.5% of its recent RS high.
